<script>
    window.onerror = function(msg, url, line, columnNo, errorObj) {
        var preventErrorAlert = true;
        var src = "";
        if (!!this.src) {
            src = "; SRC: " + this.src;
        }

        try {
            window.enhancedEcommerce.sendEvent("JS Error", msg, navigator.userAgent + " -> " + url + " : " + line + src);
        } catch (e) {
            window.console.log(e);
        }
        
        return preventErrorAlert;
    };
</script>
